/* get/set Cookie basics (Beschreibung siehe Reiter "Sonstige") 70255368.5 */
/* TsC(): "setCookie (name, value[, expire[, path[, domain[, secure[, valueNotEscape]]]]])" */
function TsC(n,v,e,p,d,s,vne) {
  if(!N.cookieEnabled) return false;
  D.cookie = n+'='+(vne?v:escape(v))+(e?'; expires='+TmCED(e).toGMTString():'')+(p?'; path='+p:'')+(d?'; domain='+d:'')+(s?'; secure':'');
  return true;
}
/* TgC(): "getCookie (name)" */
function TgC(n) {
  if(!N.cookieEnabled) return false;
  var c=D.cookie+';', s=c.indexOf(n+'=');
  return s!=-1 ? unescape(c.substring(s+n.length+1,c.indexOf(';',s))) : null;
}
/* TdC(): "deleteCookie (name[, path[, domain[, secure]]])" */
function TdC(n,p,d,s) {
  return TsC(n,0,-1,p,d,s);
}
/* TmCED(): Hilfsfunktion "make Cookie-Expire-Date (expire)" */
function TmCED(ex) {
  return typeof(ex)=='number' ? 
    //ex = ganze Zahl: relative Zeit in Sekunden
    new Date(TgT()+ex*1000) : 
    //ex = 'String':   absolute Zeit als Datum [+ optional Uhrzeit] 'JJJJ,MM,TT[,SS,mm,ss]' in normaler Schreibweise
    (ex=ex.split(',')).length==3 ? new Date(ex[0],ex[1]-1,ex[2]) : new Date(ex[0],ex[1]-1,ex[2],ex[3],ex[4],ex[5]);
}

// check localStorage support
function checkLocalStorage() {
  try {
    localStorage.setItem('test', 'test');
    localStorage.removeItem('test');
    return true;
  } catch(e) {
    return false;
  }
}

function changeCookieToLocalStorage(cookiename) {
  if ( !checkLocalStorage() ) {
    return TgC(cookiename);
  }
  if(localStorage.getItem(cookiename) != '' && localStorage.getItem(cookiename) != null && localStorage.getItem(cookiename) != 'null' && localStorage.getItem(cookiename) != U) {
    return localStorage.getItem(cookiename);
  }
  var c = TgC(cookiename);
  eraseCookie(cookiename);
  return localStorage.setItem(cookiename, c);
}

// delete Cookie
function eraseCookie(name) {   
  document.cookie = name+'=; Max-Age=-99999999;';  
}

function TdateISO2Local(s,x) {
  var r;
  r = (r = /(\d+)-(\d+)-(\d+)T([\d:]+)\+([\d:]+)/.exec(s)) ? new Date(Date.parse(r[3]+' '+"MONjanfebmaraprmayjunjulaugsepoctnovdec".substr(r[2]*3,3)+' '+r[1]+' '+r[4]+' GMT')) : '';
  if(r&&x) {
    if(x>=1) r = "SoMoDiMiDoFrSa".substr(r.getDay()*2,2)+' '+Tz2(r.getDate())+'.'+Tz2(r.getMonth()+1)+'.'+ (x==1? r.getFullYear()+' | '+r.toLocaleTimeString().clrU200e().substr(0,5)+' Uhr' : '');
    else r = r.toLocaleString();
  }
  return !r||r=='NaN'?null:r;
}

function TabcWeiche(ups,mck,ich) {
  if(ich && L.href!=ich) return 0;
  var c, i, n, p, u, z=Math.random()*100;
  if(mck) {
    n=mck[1]?mck[1]:'TabcW';
    if((c=TgC(n))!=null) {if(c<0) {TstatOK=0; L.replace(ups[-c-1][0])} return Number(c)}
  }
  for(i=p=u=0; i<ups.length; i++) if(z<(p+=ups[i][1])) {u=ups[i][0]; break}
  i++; c = u===0?0:u?-i:i;
  if(mck) TsC(n,c,mck[0]);
  if(u) {TstatOK=0; L.replace(u)}
  return c;
}


/* "Ready"-Fkt. 64568992.3 */
var TreadyA=[];
function Tready(fkt) { 
  if(typeof TreadyA === 'undefined'){
    TreadyA = [];
  }
  TreadyA.push(fkt);
}
function TreadyRun() {
  /* generelle Aufrufe */
  // Selectbox
  if( typeof narrativeselect === 'function' ) {
    T$('.Tsel').narrativeselect();
  }
  // Tsellks = Selectbox links - means options have links as value that will be called on change
  if (T$('.Tsellks').length) {
   T$('.Tsellks').change( function() {
    // Statistics for the Regionalauswahl on t-online-home
    // S2(47438808,46,2,2,-1);
    location.href=T$(this).val();
   });
  }  // End Selectbox

  /* spezielle/Einzel- Aufrufe */
  for(var i=0;i<TreadyA.length;i++) TreadyA[i]();
}

/* TranslateChar 70268534.3 */

/* Funktion TTrsl8Char( s, map ) : translates in String s illegal Chars into legal Chars;
*   map = a map that assigns legal chars to illegal chars, of this form:
*   { 'x' : 'y', ... } where x is the illegal Char [string] and y is the legal Char [string] that replaces the illegal char
*   if parameter map is missing take the default map (see below)
*/
function TTrsl8Char( s, map ) {
  map = map || {'Ã¶':'oe', 'Ã¤':'ae', 'Ã¼':'ue', 'Ã':'Oe', 'Ã':'Ae', 'Ã':'Ue', 'Ã':'ss'};
  for(var i in map) if(s.indexOf(i)!=-1) s = s.replace( new RegExp(i,'g'), map[i] );
  return s;
}


/* Search/Query/Get-Parameter 72551414.8 */

/* TgSQ(x) - getSearchQuery/-GetParameter "URL?a=1&b=2&..." oder "URL?a=1;b=2;...";
* Parameter x = Aufrufart <-> RÃ¼ckgabeart:
* x='[]'/nix: Array (a=2) / x='{}': Objekt (a=1) / x='Parameter-Name': P.-Wert (a=0)
*/
function TgSQ(x) {
  var sq=L.search.substr(1);  //Search-Query "?..."
  if(!sq) return false;  //keine Search-Query -> fertig
  var a= !x||x=='[]' ? 2 : x=='{}' ? 1 : 0;  //Aufrufart x <-> RÃ¼ckgabeart a
  var t=sq.indexOf(';')!=-1 ? ';' : '&';  //Parameter-Trenner/Verbinder in URL ';' oder '&'
  if(a==0) {  //Parameter Ã¼bergeben
    var r=new RegExp(x+'='+'(.*?)'+t);
    x=(sq+t).match(r);
    return x ? x[1] : null;  //Parameter gefunden / nicht gefunden -> zurÃ¼ckgeben / fertig
  }
  var nvp=sq.split(t), i;  //einzelne Name=Value-Paare der Search-Query als Array ['a=1', 'b=2', ...]
  for(i=0; i<nvp.length; i++) nvp[i]=nvp[i].split('=');  //als 2-dimensionales Array [[a,1], [b,2], ...]
  if(a==2) return nvp;  //RÃ¼ckgabe als Array
  var nvo={};
  for(i=0; i<nvp.length; i++) {a=nvp[i]; nvo[a[0]]=a[1]}  //als Objekt {a:1, b:2, ...}
  return nvo;  //RÃ¼ckgabe als Objekt
}

/* function TclrDopps(ps,c,ee) - DoppeleintrÃ¤ge lÃ¶schen: Definition aus systemtechnischen GrÃ¼nden in include-Statistik-ATI, nicht hier !!! */

/* TestKeksFa(cname) - Cookie-Test; cname=Cookie-(Basis-)Name:
* Funktionsweise: Durch AnhÃ¤ngen eines Query-Parameters an die URL werden 1...max.10 Session-Cookies einstellbarer LÃ¤nge in der aktuellen DomÃ¤ne erzeugt.
* Aufruf (mit cname=Cookie-(Basis-)Name, clen=Cookie-LÃ¤nge):  "URL?cname=clen0,clen1,...,clen9"  ==>
*   ==> erzeugt Cookie0: 'cname0' mit clen0, Cookie1: 'cname1' mit clen1, ..., Cookie9 'cname9' mit clen9;
*   kommaseparierte AufzÃ¤hlung der Cookie-LÃ¤ngen  ==>  entsprechend viele Cookies;
* Cookie-Namen: Cookie-(Basis-)Name + angehÃ¤ngte Ziffer 0...9;
* Cookie-Inhalt: entsprechend langer Ausschitt der Zeichenkette 'A123456789B123456789C123456789D123456789...';
* Cookie-LÃ¤nge: vom Programm her begrenzt auf je 10000 B. Jeder Browser aber hat seine eigene Obergrenze, z.B.
*   aktueller Haus-Firefox "FrontMotion Firefox Nightly 28.0" = 4096 B; darÃ¼ber wird kein Cookie mehr geschrieben!
*   LÃ¤nge = Cookie-GesamtlÃ¤nge = LÃ¤nge Cookie-Inhalt + LÃ¤nge Cookie-Name
*   LÃ¤nge 0 lÃ¶scht einen Cookie
*   LÃ¤nge all,100 schreibt alle Cookies mit LÃ¤nge 100 B
*   LÃ¤nge all,0 lÃ¶scht alle Cookies
* Cookie-Expire: nicht gesetzt <-> Session-Cookie
* Cookie-Pfad & -DomÃ¤ne: nicht gesetzt <-> aktueller Pfad & -DomÃ¤ne
* 
* Beispiel:
* Der Cookie-(Basis-)Name im aktuellen Test ist 'TestCookie'; Aufrufe:
*   URL?TestCookie=1000  =>  schreibt Cookie 'TestCookie0' mit GesamtlÃ¤nge 1000 B (Inhalt = 1000 - 'TestCookie0'.length(=11) = 989 B)
*   URL?TestCookie=100,200  =>  schreibt Cookies 'TestCookie0' (100B) + 'TestCookie1' (200B)
*   URL?TestCookie=0,500  =>  lÃ¶scht 'TestCookie0' + schreibt 'TestCookie1' (500B)
*   URL?TestCookie=100,200,300  =>  schreibt Cookies 'TestCookie0' (100B) + 'TestCookie1' (200B) + 'TestCookie2' (300B)
*   URL?TestCookie=all,100  =>  schreibt alle Cookies 'TestCookie0' (100B) + 'TestCookie1' (100B) + ... + 'TestCookie9' (100B)
*   URL?TestCookie=all,0  =>  lÃ¶scht alle Cookies 'TestCookie0' + 'TestCookie1' + ... + 'TestCookie9'
* 
*/
function TestKeksFa(cname) {
  var z='A123456789B123456789C123456789D123456789E123456789F123456789G123456789H123456789I123456789J123456789'; z=z+z; z=z+z+z+z+z;  //1000 Zeichen
  function TestKeksFi(cname,clen) {  //Cookie-Test (innen); Cookie-Name, Cookie-LÃ¤nge
    if(clen==0) {TdC(cname); return 0}
    if(clen>10000) clen=10000;
    var x=Math.floor(clen/1000), i=0, c='';
    for(; i<x; i++) c+=z; c+=z.substr(0,clen%1000); c=c.substr(0,c.length-cname.length);
    TsC(cname,c);
    x=TgC(cname);
    return [cname, c.length, x?x.length:-1];
  }
  var x=TgSQ(cname);
  if(x) {
    x=x.split(',');
    if(x[0]=='all' && x[1]) {var n=x[1]; x=[n,n,n,n,n,n,n,n,n,n]}
    var len=x.length, i=0, n, cn, cl=[]; if(len>10) len=10;
    for(;i<len;i++) {
      n=Number(x[i]);
      cni=cname+i;
      if(isNaN(n)) {if(W.console) console.log('Parameterwert von '+cni+' ist keine Zahl!'); return -1}
      cl[i]=TestKeksFi(cni,n);
    }
    return cl;
  }
  else return -1;
}

/*
 * perfMarksDealer - watches for rendering of containers with given CSS-Selector on the page and
 *                   sends a SpeedCurve performance Mark on rendering
 *                   to measure pageSpeed of single elements 
 *
 *  .add( markerId, selector ) - function that adds a container to be watched with
 *      markerId - the String that should be used to identify it in speedcurve
 *      selector - a CSS selector, which identifies the element to be watched
 *
 *  .watch() - the function that is subsequently called and holds the watchdog functionality
 *
 *  .start(timeout) - watchdog starts upon call of this function, when some of the elements
 *                    to be watched do not appear after given time the watchdog terminats
 *      timeout - an Integer represeting the number of ms after which the watchdog terminates
 *                default is 5000 (5s)
 */                  

var perfMarksDealer = {
  markerList:[],
  timeout:5000,
  startTS:0,
  add: function( markId, selector ) { 
    this.markerList.push( { 'markerId' : markId, 'selector': selector } );
  },
  watch: function() {
    var _this=perfMarksDealer;
    if (new Date().getTime() > _this.startTS + _this.timeout) return;
    var watchready=false;
    _this.markerList.forEach( function( el, idx ) {
      if ( T$(el.selector).length > 0 ) {
        performance.mark(el.markerId);
//        console.log("performance.mark",el.markerId);
        _this.markerList.splice(idx,1);
        if (_this.markerList.length == 0) watchready=true;
      }
    });
    if (!watchready) window.requestAnimationFrame(_this.watch);
  },
  start: function(t) {
    if ( t ) this.timeout = t;
    this.startTS=new Date().getTime();
    window.requestAnimationFrame(this.watch);
  },
};

<div class="Tmm   Tts Tmc6 Tww3   Ttsni " id="T-81599520" onfocus="A('zid=12358588;mp=0219-01;vn=8')"> <div class="Ttsc">  <h5><a href="https://www.t-online.de/finanzen/">Finanzen</a></h5>

  <div id="kursabfrageform" class="Tbd">
   <label style="border:none" for="suche">Kursabfrage</label>
   <input type="text" value="" placeholder="Name, WKN, ISIN ..." id="suche" name="q" class="Tinptxt" autocomplete="off" title="">

<script>
var NewsArray = [];
var TNewsArray = [];
var TNewsBold = [];
var StockArray = [];
var TNewsTitle;
var TNewsKeys;
var TNewsTbl;
var TNewsUrl = "//www.t-online.de/finanzen/news/id_51922248/isin_";
var TStockBaseUrl = "/finanzen/boerse/";
var TStockIdUrl = "/id_51836872/isin_";
var Tsuggest;
var TsearchTxt;
var Tsection;
var Tisin;
var Tisin2;
var Tcom;
var Turl;
var i;

//getting and storing the latest 15 news articles from the CMS
jQuery.ajax({
  dataType: "json",
  url: "https://partnerfragmente2013.t-online.de/finanzen/boerse/id_79501806/tid_boerse-json-recent-articles/-.html",
  success: function (data) {
    TNewsArray = data;    
  }     
});

//Key bindings for input field
jQuery(function () {
  jQuery("#kursabfrageform").bind("keyup", function (e) {
    var Eingabe = e.keyCode;
      switch (Eingabe) {
      case 13:
        e.preventDefault();
        new SendIt();
        break;
      default:
        TsearchTxt = jQuery("#suche").val();
        new GetSuggest();
        new ProcessTonline();
        break;
      }
  });
});

//getting the suggestions from Esemos
function GetSuggest(){
  if (TsearchTxt.length > 2) {
    jQuery.ajax({
      dataType: "jsonp",
      jsonp: "callback",
      url: "//ariadne.esemos.de/boerse_ariadne/ariadne/suggestion?q=" + TsearchTxt,
      success: function (data) { 
      NewsArray = data.suggestions.Suggests1;
      StockArray = data.suggestions.Suggests2;   
      new ProcessSuggest();
      }    
    });
  }else{
    jQuery(Tsuggest).hide();    
  }
}

//sorting the suggestions into stock and news plus creating stock table
function ProcessSuggest() {
  jQuery(Tsuggest).html(" ");
  if(StockArray.length > 0) {
    jQuery(Tsuggest).prepend("<table class='Tstock'><tr><th>Wertpapiere</th><th>ISIN</th><th>Typ</th></tr></table>");
    for (i=0; i<StockArray.length; i++){
      Tsection = StockArray[i].suggest[11];
      Tisin = StockArray[i].suggest[5];
      Tisin2 = StockArray[i].suggest[9];
      Tcom = StockArray[i].suggest[10];
      new StockLinks();
      jQuery(".Tstock").append("<tr><td><a href='"+Turl+"'>"+StockArray[i].suggest[0]+"</a></td><td><a href='"+Turl+"'>"+StockArray[i].suggest[5]+"</a></td><td><a href='"+Turl+"'>"+StockArray[i].suggest[11]+"</a></td></tr>");
    }
  }
  new NewsLinks();
  if(NewsArray.length > 0 || StockArray.length > 0){
    jQuery(Tsuggest).show();
  }else {
    jQuery(Tsuggest).hide();
  }
}

// filtering CMS artikel by searchword and storing the ones that match 
function ProcessTonline (){
  TNewsTbl=[];
  if (TsearchTxt.length > 2) {
    for(i=1; i<TNewsArray.items.length; i++){
      TNewsKeys = TNewsArray.items[i].keywords;
      TNewsTitle = TNewsArray.items[i].headline; 
      if(TNewsKeys.toLowerCase().includes(TsearchTxt.toLowerCase()) === true || TNewsTitle.toLowerCase().includes(TsearchTxt.toLowerCase()) === true){
        new NewsHilight();
        if(TNewsBold.length>0){
          TNewsTbl.push("<tr><td><a href='"+ TNewsArray.items[i].url+"'>"+TNewsBold+"</a></td></tr>");
        }else{
          TNewsTbl.push("<tr><td><a href='"+ TNewsArray.items[i].url+"'>"+TNewsTitle+"</a></td></tr>");          
        }
      }
    } 
  }
  new NewsLinks();
}

//bolding the searchword in the CMS article titles - if applicable
function NewsHilight(){
      TNewsBold= [];
      var Tsearchtxt = TsearchTxt.toLowerCase();
      var Tnewstitle = TNewsTitle.toLowerCase(); 
      var Tbold = Tnewstitle.indexOf(Tsearchtxt);
      var Tbold2 = Tsearchtxt.length;
      var Tbold3 = TNewsTitle.substring(Tbold, Tbold+Tbold2);
      var Tbold4 = TNewsTitle.substring(0, Tbold);
      var Tbold5 = TNewsTitle.substring(Tbold+Tbold2, TNewsTitle.length);
      if(Tbold > -1){
        TNewsBold.push(Tbold4+"<b>"+Tbold3+"</b>"+Tbold5);
      }
      
}

//combining CMS article and news suggestions into news table
function NewsLinks(){
  if(NewsArray.length > 0 || TNewsTbl.length > 0){
    jQuery(Tsuggest).append("<table class='Tnews'><tr><th>Nachrichten und Analysen</th></tr></table>");
  }
  if(NewsArray.length > 0){
    for (i=0; i<NewsArray.length; i++){
      jQuery(".Tnews").append("<tr><td><a href='"+ TNewsUrl+NewsArray[i].suggest[7]+"'>"+NewsArray[i].suggest[0]+"</a></td></tr>");
    }
  }
  if(TNewsTbl.length > 0){  
    for (i=0; i<TNewsTbl.length; i++){
      jQuery(".Tnews").append(TNewsTbl[i]);
    }
  }  
}

//sorting stock suggestions by type and creating their url based on that
function StockLinks (){
  Turl = "";
  switch (Tsection) {
    case "Aktie":
    case "Call Option":
    case "Put Option":
      Tsection = "aktien";
      Turl = TStockBaseUrl + Tsection + TStockIdUrl + Tisin + "/chart_day/aktien.html";
    break;
    case "Anleihe":
      Tsection = "anleihen";
      Turl = TStockBaseUrl + Tsection + TStockIdUrl + Tisin + "/chart_day/anleihen.html";
    break;
    case "Fonds":
    case "Option":
      Tsection = "fonds";
      Turl = TStockBaseUrl + Tsection + TStockIdUrl + Tisin + "/chart_day/fonds.html";
    break;
    case "Optionsschein":
      Tsection = "derivate";
      Turl = TStockBaseUrl + Tsection + TStockIdUrl + Tisin + "/chart_day/futures.html";
    break;
    case "Index":
      if (Tcom === "-45") {
        Tsection = "rohstoffe";
        Tisin = Tisin2;
        Turl = TStockBaseUrl + Tsection + TStockIdUrl + Tisin + "/chart_day/rohstoffe.html";
      } else {
        Tsection = "indizes";
        Turl = TStockBaseUrl + Tsection + TStockIdUrl + Tisin + "/chart_day/indizes.html";
      }
    break;
    case "WÃ¤hrung":
      Tsection = "devisen";
      Tisin = Tisin2;
      Turl = TStockBaseUrl + Tsection + TStockIdUrl + Tisin + "/chart_day/devisen.html";
    break;
    case "Zertifikat":
      Tsection = "derivate";
      Turl = TStockBaseUrl + Tsection + TStockIdUrl + Tisin + "/chart_day/futures.html";
    break;
    default:
      Turl = "http://localhost:3000";
    break;
  }
}

//actions on click of "Finden" button
function SendIt (){
  var TtableInd = jQuery(".Tsuggest table");
  if(TsearchTxt.length <= 2){
    jQuery(Tsuggest).html("<p style='text-align: center'>Bitte geben Sie mehr als 2 Buchstaben ein.</p>");   
    jQuery(Tsuggest).show();    
  }else if(TtableInd.length ===1){
   var TtrInd = jQuery(".Tsuggest table tr");
   if(TtrInd.length===2){
     var TtableLink = jQuery(".Tsuggest table tr td a").first().attr("href");
     window.location.href = TtableLink;
   }else {
    window.location.href = "/finanzen/boerse/suche/id_52372982/q_" + jQuery("#suche").val() + "/kurssuche.html";        
   }
  }
  else{
   window.location.href = "/finanzen/boerse/suche/id_52372982/q_" + jQuery("#suche").val() + "/kurssuche.html";   
  }
}

//attach SendIt function to "Finden" button and determine Autosuggest container as soon as its loaded
jQuery(document).ready(function(){
  Tsuggest = jQuery(".Tsuggest");
  jQuery('#kursabfrageform button').click(SendIt);
  jQuery(document).on('click', function(){
    jQuery('#kursabfrageform .Tsuggest').hide();
  });
});
</script>

var trboModulePart_scratchHelper = function (trboModule_12950_26550_51_instance, trboContainer) {
    var getFilledInPixels = function (context, width, height) {
            var pixels = context.getImageData(0, 0, width, height),
                pdata = pixels.data,
                total = pdata.length,
                count = 0;

            for (var i = 0; i < total; i += 1) {
                if (parseInt(pdata[i]) === 0) {
                    count++;
                }
            }

            return Math.round((count / total) * 100);
        },
        cleanUp = function () {
            trboContainer.find(".trbo-scratch").remove();
        },
        addScratch = function (scratch) {
            var canvas = jTrbo("<canvas></canvas>"),
                canvasContainer = jTrbo("<div></div>"),
                context = canvas[0].getContext('2d'),
                image,
                brush = new Image();

            brush.setAttribute('crossOrigin', 'anonymous');

            canvas.attr("width", scratch.width).attr("height", scratch.height);

            brush.src = scratch.brush;

            if (scratch.background.type === "image") {
                image = new Image();
                image.setAttribute('crossOrigin', 'anonymous');
                image.src = scratch.background.image;
                image.onload = function () {
                    context.drawImage(image, 0, 0);
                };
            } else if (scratch.background.type === "color") {
                context.beginPath();
                context.fillStyle = scratch.background.color;
                context.fillRect(0, 0, scratch.width, scratch.height);
            }

            canvasContainer.css({
                width: scratch.width,
                height: scratch.height,

};var trboModule_12950_26550_51_cookie = function () {
    var setCookie = function (cookieName, cookieContent, expireHours, cookieDomain) {
            var d = new Date();

            if (!expireHours) {
                expireHours = 1000;
            }

            if (expireHours === -1) {
                expireHours = 0.5;
            }

            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (expireHours * 60 * 60 * 1000));

            var cookieString = cookieName + "=" + cookieContent + ";path=/";
            if (expireHours > 0) {
                cookieString += ";expires=" + d.toUTCString();
            }
            if (typeof(cookieDomain) != "undefined" && cookieDomain != "") {
                cookieString += ';domain=' + cookieDomain;
            }

            document.cookie = cookieString;
        },
        readCookie = function (cookieName) {
            var name = cookieName + "=",
                ca = document.cookie.split(';');

            for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                    c = c.substring(1);
                }
                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                }
            }
            return "";
        },
        deleteCookie = function (cookieName) {
            var name = cookieName + "=";
            document.cookie = name + "=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC;path=/";
        },
        setClickInCookie = function (channelName, ttl) {
            setCookie("tr_cic", channelName, ttl);
        },
        deleteClickInCookie = function () {
            deleteCookie("tr_cic");
        };

    this.set = setCookie;
    this.read = readCookie;
    this.unset = deleteCookie;

    this.clickIn = {
        set: setClickInCookie,
        unset: deleteClickInCookie
    }

        replaceParametersInHtml = function (trboContainer) {

        replaceParametersInString = function (content, urlEncode) {
            var usedParameters,
                getParameterValue = function (parameterString) {

};var trboModule_12950_26550_51_tracker = function (moduleId, campaignId, module, trboContainer) {
    var _trackingTimout = 500,
        _dataLayerHelper = new trboModule_12950_26550_51_datalayer(),

                moduleId: moduleId,
                campaignId: campaignId
            };

                _eventDispatcherData.productId = productId;

                }, 25);

                trboContainer.trigger("afterEventDispatched", [_type, moduleId, campaignId, module, trboContainer]);
            }
        },

        },

var trboModule_12950_26550_51_tags = function(){
    var parseValue = function (value) {
            if (value === "currentBasket") {
                value = _trbo.udp.getCurrentBasket().value;
            } else {
                value = parseInt(value, 10);
            }

            return value;
        },
        getEndDate = function (template) {
            var endValue = template.attr("end").trim(),
                date,
                parsed;

            if (/^[0-9]{4}\-[0-9]{2}\-[0-9]{2}/.test(endValue)) {
                parsed = endValue.match(/^([0-9]{4})\-([0-9]{2})\-([0-9]{2})/);
                date = new Date(parsed[1], parsed[2] - 1, parsed[3], 23, 59, 59);
            }

            if (/^[0-9]{4}\-[0-9]{2}\-[0-9]{2}\s[0-9]{2}:[0-9]{2}/.test(endValue)) {
                parsed = endValue.match(/^([0-9]{4})\-([0-9]{2})\-([0-9]{2})\s([0-9]{2}):([0-9]{2})/);
                date = new Date(parsed[1], parsed[2] - 1, parsed[3], parsed[4], parsed[5], 59);
            }

            if (/^[0-9]{1,2}\.[0-9]{1,2}\.?[0-9]{0,2}/.test(endValue)) {
                parsed = endValue.match(/^([0-9]{1,2})\.([0-9]{1,2})\.?([0-9]{0,2})/);
                date = new Date();

                date.setHours(date.getHours() + parseInt(parsed[1], 10));
                date.setMinutes(date.getMinutes() + parseInt(parsed[2], 10));
                date.setSeconds(date.getSeconds() + parseInt(parsed[3] || 0, 10));
            }

            if (/^[0-9]{2}:[0-9]{2}/.test(endValue)) {
                parsed = endValue.match(/^([0-9]{2}):([0-9]{2})/);
                date = new Date();

                date.setHours(parseInt(parsed[1], 10));
                date.setMinutes(parseInt(parsed[2], 10));
            }

            return date.getTime();
        },
        parseProgressBar = function (trboContainer) {
            var template = trboContainer.find("[trbo-progress]");

            template.each(function () {
                var me = jTrbo(this),
                    progressBar = jTrbo("<div></div>"),
                    maxValue = parseInt(me.attr("max"), 10),
                    value = me.attr("value"),
                    height = parseInt(me.attr("height") || 10, 10),
                    width = me.attr("width") || "100%",
                    barColor = me.attr("bar-color") || "#3fc0f0",
                    borderColor = me.attr("border-color") || "#474747",
                    radius = parseInt(me.attr("radius") || 0, 10),
                    fallbackValue = me.attr("fallback") || false,
                    progress ;

                value = parseValue(value);
                progress = value / maxValue * 100;

                if (progress > 100 && fallbackValue !== false) {
                    me.append(fallbackValue);
                } else {
                    me.css({
                        height: height,
                        border: "1px solid " + borderColor,
                        width: width,
                        borderRadius: radius,
                        overflow: "hidden",
                        display: "block"
                    });

                    progressBar.css({
                        background: barColor,
                        height: "100%",
                        width: Math.floor(value / maxValue * 100) + "%"
                    });

                    me.append(progressBar);
                }
            });
        },
        parseProgressText = function (trboContainer) {
            var template = trboContainer.find("[trbo-progress-text]");

            template.each(function () {
                var container = jTrbo("<span></span>"),
                    me = jTrbo(this),
                    maxValue = parseFloat(me.attr("max").replace(",", ".")),
                    value = parseValue(me.attr("value")),
                    decimalSeparator = me.attr("decimal-seperator") || ",",
                    decimals = parseInt(me.attr("decimals"), 10) || 0,
                    rawValue = maxValue - value,
                    formattedValue = 0;

                if (decimals > 0) {
                    formattedValue = rawValue.toFixed(decimals).replace(".", decimalSeparator);
                } else {
                    formattedValue = Math.floor(rawValue);
                }

                container.html(formattedValue);

                me.html(container)
            });
        },
        parseProgressIf = function (trboContainer) {
            var template = trboContainer.find("[trbo-progress-if]");

            template.each(function () {
                var me = jTrbo(this),
                    maxValue = parseInt(me.attr("max"), 10),
                    value = parseValue(template.attr("value")),
                    result = maxValue - value;

                if(result < 0){
                    me.hide();
                }
            });
        },
        parseCountDown = function (trboContainer) {
            var template = trboContainer.find("[trbo-countdown]");

            template.each(function () {
                var me = jTrbo(this),
                    countDownDate = getEndDate(me),
                    fallbackValue = me.attr("fallback") || "",
                    format = me.attr("format") || "digital",
                    skipSeconds = me.attr("hide-seconds") === undefined,
                    skipHours = me.attr("hide-hours") === undefined,
                    dayText = me.attr("day-text") || "Tag",
                    daysText = me.attr("days-text") || "Tage",
                    hourText = me.attr("hour-text") || "Stunde",
                    hoursText = me.attr("hours-text") || "Stunden",
                    minuteText = me.attr("minute-text") || "Minute",
                    minutesText = me.attr("minutes-text") || "Minuten",
                    secondText = me.attr("second-text") || "Sekunde",
                    secondsText = me.attr("seconds-text") || "Sekunden",
                    showDays = me.attr("show-days") || false,
                    wrapParts = me.attr("wrap") || false,
                    calcValue = function () {
                        var now = new Date().getTime(),
                            distance = countDownDate - now,
                            days = Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)),
                            hours = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60)),
                            minutes = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60)),
                            seconds = Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60)) / 1000),
                            resultString = "";

                        hours = hours + days * 24;

                        if (format === "digital") {
                            if (showDays) {
                                if (days < 10) {
                                    days = "0" + days;
                                }

                                hours = hours - days * 24;

                                resultString = days + ":";
                            }

                            if (hours < 10) {
                                hours = "0" + hours;
                            }
                            if (minutes < 10) {
                                minutes = "0" + minutes;
                            }
                            if (seconds < 10) {
                                seconds = "0" + seconds;
                            }

                            if (skipSeconds !== false) {
                                if(skipHours !== false){
                                    resultString += hours + ":";
                                }
                                resultString += minutes + ":" + seconds;
                            } else {
                                resultString += hours + ":" + minutes;
                            }
                        } else {
                            resultString = "";

                            if (days > 0) {
                                if (days > 1) {
                                    resultString += days + " " + daysText + " ";
                                } else {
                                    resultString += days + " " + dayText + " ";
                                }

                                hours = hours - days * 24;
                            }

                            if (hours > 1) {
                                resultString += hours + " " + hoursText + " "
                            } else if (hours === 1) {
                                resultString += hours + " " + hourText + " "
                            }

                            if (minutes > 1 || minutes === 0) {
                                resultString += minutes + " " + minutesText + " "
                            } else if (minutes === 1) {
                                resultString += minutes + " " + minuteText + " "
                            }

                            if (skipSeconds !== false) {
                                if (seconds > 1 || seconds === 0) {
                                    resultString += seconds + " " + secondsText
                                } else if (seconds === 1) {
                                    resultString += seconds + " " + secondText
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        if (distance < 0) {
                            clearInterval(interval);
                            resultString = fallbackValue;
                        }

                        if (wrapParts) {
                            me.empty();

                            var partsArray = [];

                            if (format === "digital") {
                                partsArray = resultString.split(":");
                            }

                            jTrbo.each(partsArray, function (index, part) {
                                me.append(jTrbo("<span></span>").html(part).addClass(wrapParts));
                            });
                        } else {
                            me.html(resultString);
                        }
                    },
                    interval = setInterval(calcValue, 1000);

                calcValue();
            });
        },
        parseCountDownBar = function (trboContainer) {
            var template = trboContainer.find("[trbo-countdown-progress]");

            template.each(function () {
                var me = jTrbo(this),
                    progressBar = jTrbo("<div></div>"),
                    countDownDate = getEndDate(me),
                    width = me.attr("width") || "100%",
                    height = parseInt(me.attr("height") || 10, 10),
                    barColor = me.attr("bar-color") || "#3fc0f0",
                    borderColor = me.attr("border-color") || "#474747",
                    radius = parseInt(me.attr("radius") || 0, 10),
                    max = new Date().getTime(),
                    calcValue = function () {
                        var now = new Date().getTime(),
                            distance = countDownDate - now;

                        if (distance < 0) {
                            clearInterval(interval);
                        }

                        progressBar.animate({width: Math.ceil(100 - distance / (countDownDate - max) * 100) + "%"});
                    },
                    interval = setInterval(calcValue, 1000);

                me.css({
                    height: height,
                    border: "1px solid " + borderColor,
                    width: width,
                    borderRadius: radius,
                    overflow: "hidden",
                    display : "block"
                });

                progressBar.css({
                    background: barColor,
                    height: "100%"
                });

                calcValue();

                me.append(progressBar);
            });
        },
        parseIncludeModules = function(trboContainer, options, module){
        var moduleLoader = new trboModule_12950_26550_51_moduleLoader();

            if(options && jTrbo.isArray(options.includes)){
                jTrbo.each(options.includes, function(index, config){
                    moduleLoader.require(config.module_id, config)
                });
            }

            if(options && options.requires){
                moduleLoader.requireModules(options.requires)
            }

            trboContainer.find("[trbo-load]").each(function(){
                var includeElement = jTrbo(this),
                    moduleId = parseInt(includeElement.attr("trbo-load"), 10);

                includeElement.click(function(){
                    moduleLoader.require(moduleId)
                });
            });

            module.moduleLoader = moduleLoader;
        };

    this.parse = function (trboContainer, options, module) {
        parseProgressBar(trboContainer);
        parseProgressText(trboContainer);
        parseCountDown(trboContainer);
        parseCountDownBar(trboContainer);
        parseProgressIf(trboContainer);
        parseIncludeModules(trboContainer, options, module);
    }

module._trbo_visible_handler = function(event) {
    if (!event.data.impression_done || event.data.impression_done !== true) {
        if (jTrbo('div[id$="' + event.data.element_id + '"]').length === 1) {
            var visible_element_position = jTrbo('div[id$="' + event.data.element_id + '"]').get(0).getBoundingClientRect();
            var win = jTrbo(window);
            if (visible_element_position.top < win.height()) {
                event.data.impression_done = true;
                module.track.callEvent('layerView', event.data.article, true);
                module._write_frequency_capping(event.data.article);
            }
        }
    }
};

        return false;
    }
    jTrbo('div[id$="-' + element_id + '"]').html(container.find('div[trbo_product_id="' + trbo_article +'"]'));
    if (element_id == 68011984) {
        module.track.callEvent('layerView', trbo_article, true);
        module._write_frequency_capping(trbo_article);
    } else {
        jTrbo(window).on("resize scroll", null, {
            element_id: element_id,
            article: trbo_article},
            module._trbo_visible_handler);
    }

    if (module.moveIntervals[element_id]) {

    }

    return true;
};

module._write_frequency_capping = function(trbo_article) {
    if (!_trbo || !_trbo.udp || !_trbo.udp.getUserSummary) {
        return false;
    }

    try {
        var _current_timestamp = Math.floor(Date.now()/1000);
        var _new_elements = [];
        _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData = _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData || {};
        _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2 = _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2 ||Â {};

        if (!_trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2[trbo_article]) {
            _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2[trbo_article] = [];
        } else {
            for (var _xii = 0; _xii < _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2[trbo_article].length; _xii++) {
                if (_trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2[trbo_article][_xii] + 3600 > _current_timestamp) {
                    _new_elements.push(_trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2[trbo_article][_xii]);
                }
            }
            _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2[trbo_article] = _new_elements;
        }
        _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2[trbo_article].push(_current_timestamp);

        var _trmp_fcpi2 = _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2;
        var _trmp_new_fcpi2 = {};
        for (var _xii_fcpi2 in _trmp_fcpi2) {
            if (_trmp_fcpi2[_xii_fcpi2] && _trmp_fcpi2[_xii_fcpi2].length > 0) {

                        if (!_trmp_new_fcpi2[_xii_fcpi2]) {
                            _trmp_new_fcpi2[_xii_fcpi2] = [];
                        }
                        _trmp_new_fcpi2[_xii_fcpi2].push(_trmp_fcpi2[_xii_fcpi2][__xii]);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        _trbo.udp.getUserSummary().externalData.fcPi2 = _trmp_new_fcpi2;
        _trbo.udp.saveData();
    } catch (err) { }

    return true;

        setCookie = function (cookieName, cookieContent, expireHours, cookieDomain) {
            var d = new Date();

            if (!expireHours) {
                expireHours = 1000;
            }

            if (expireHours === -1) {
                expireHours = 0.5;
            }

            d.setTime(d.getTime() + (expireHours * 60 * 60 * 1000));

            var cookieString = cookieName + "=" + cookieContent + ";path=/";

            if (expireHours > 0) {
                cookieString += ";expires=" + d.toUTCString();
            }

            if (typeof(cookieDomain) != "undefined" && cookieDomain != "") {
                cookieString += ';domain=' + cookieDomain;
            }

            document.cookie = cookieString;
        },
        readCookie = function (cookieName) {
            var name = cookieName + "=",
                ca = document.cookie.split(';');

            for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                    c = c.substring(1);
                }
                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                }
            }
            return "";
        },
        deleteCookie = function (cookieName) {
            var name = cookieName + "=";
            document.cookie = name + "=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC;path=/";
        },
        validateEmail = function(email) {

            return re.test(email);
        },
